# Text Elements
Meem with and without sukoon
 ^TBjscYOX

Meem Sakinah ^qvwbewxQ

[[Clear Meem]] ^GzJno4TW

A clear meem is really easy because just like noon,
a clear meem is a meem that has sukoon on it (so if it
doesn't have a sukoon, then). ^Kb6c3bSQ

[[Merging Meem]] ^IAd0G4L2

This is also really easy. Again just like noon, you have to extend
the ghunnah for 1 second, except the only letter for Merging Meem
is Meem! 
- And again, just like Noon Sakinah, if a meem has a shaddah, extend
ghunnah for 1 second as well ^53Ro4EQJ

[[Hiding Meem]] ^H8H3h3ej

Hiding meem is when the meem is proceeded by a 'ba'. So when going into the meem,
your mouth is open, and when going in to the 'ba' your mouth is also open. But in the middle,
while your still pronouncing the 'mmm' sound, extend ghunnah for 1 second ^WRBeKenN

MOUTH ^7Q1jgFZY

STATUS ^9vbBuyR2

%%
